  Cheese sandwich recipe | चीज़ सैंडविच कैसे बनता है  | Cheese sandwich street food style | Delicious Pakwan

This is one of our favorite breakfast and snack for Evening. It does not take much time and effort to make these delicious cheese sandwiches. 

Preparation Time: 15 minutes

Ingredients:
1. Fresh slices of bread
2. Butter as required (1 tbsp)
3. Cheese as required
4. Capsicums (Red, Green, Yellow)
5. Oregano 
6. Mayonnaise
7. Tomato Sauce

  Bread ka meetha, also known as&nbsp;Shahi Tukra,is a&nbsp;bread pudding&nbsp;Indian sweet&nbsp;of fried bread slices soaked in hot&nbsp;milk&nbsp;with spices,including&nbsp;saffron&nbsp;and&nbsp;cardamom.Bread  ka meetha is a&nbsp;dessert&nbsp;of&nbsp;Hyderabad, Telangana.&nbsp;It is popular in&nbsp;Hyderabadi cuisine, served at&nbsp;weddings&nbsp;and parties. Bread ka meetha refers to the milk bread, called "Double Roti" in the local Indian dialects because it swells up to almost double its original size after baking.
